‚Äî‚ÄîThe most important point is here: 1. Room hardware, software, what a gadget, not to mention a little distance from the five-star, it can be said to be completely irrelevant! ! ! In Hainan for more than ten days, staying in a Wyndham brand hotel, the room is almost a 3-star configuration, the bathing place is equipped with such a shower curtain, which five-star hotel I have seen! ? Needless to say, the decoration of the room, the style and taste, the bed is hard and small, and a bench can be used as furniture. The balcony seats are still painted, which is quite 3 stars.
  After checking, it turned out that it was not designed and decorated by Wyndham brand before. It is estimated that this year's epidemic affected the hotel and the hotel could not hold it. Wyndham became a shareholder and managed it. No wonder the hardware facilities are so bad! ! Really for the first time in a 5-star hotel in Hainan without ice and ice buckets.
  This time I was really disappointed with the Wyndham brand. I was completely disappointed. I took over a hotel that could not be managed and thought it was a bargain. I trouble to consider the positioning of my own brand.
  Compared with the Wyndham Grand Palace on Qinglan Peninsula across the sea, this is the standard Wyndham should have. The hotel is not only about service, but also about the experience of rooms and facilities. The price is very 5-star, but the hardware is absolutely quasi 3-star. Compared with many five-star hotels in Hainan, it can be said to be the worst, none of them! !

In addition, I seriously suspect that the hotel rating of Ctrip has been recharged. It is actually higher than the nearby Jinshi International, and the search ranks first. What's so good about it? The 5-star level of software and hardware in this room ranks Wenchang first. Ctrip also trouble to pay attention to the absence of the hotel. Wyndham Garden is completely a typical pick-up hotel among the golden jade, and it is not worth the experience at this price! !
  Therefore, I advise you to come to Wenchang to experience a quiet hotel vacation. The first choice is Jinshi International and Wyndham Grand Plaza, two truly five-star hotels. The prices are completely worthy of all aspects. As for Wyndham Garden, it looks like this. There is no way to survive, the entire hotel design is not at all standard, except for those who want to enjoy the invincible sea view, the price is about 300 to experience.
  ps: In terms of service and management, Wyndham's intervention is still passable. This is worthy of recognition, but there is nothing else.
